### OSS_REPORT.md

# OSS Harvest Report — Autonomous Agents Reliability Hardening v1.0

**Date**: 2026-03-18
**Target**: DanteCode Autonomous Agents Reliability Score 6.8 → 8+
**Focus**: Checkpoint/resume, circuit-breaker, recovery-engine, stuck-loop detection

## Repos Scanned

| Repo | License | Stars | Relevant Patterns |

## DanteForge Pipeline

### Specification Refinement
- Zero-ambiguity templates for constitution, specs, plans, and tasks
- Clarification engine for detecting gaps and inconsistencies
- Constitution enforcement on every phase transition

### Execution Waves
- Atomic wave execution with structured prompts
- Phase-based task sequencing with verification loops
- Profile-adaptive: quality | balanced | budget

### Multi-Agent Orchestration
- PM, Architect, Dev, UX, Scrum Master agent roles
- Party Mode for scale-adaptive multi-agent collaboration
- Parallel execution with git worktree isolation

## Recommended Next Steps
1. Run `danteforge constitution` to establish project principles and enforcement rules
2. Run `danteforge specify "<goal>"` to create spec artifacts from this review
3. Run `danteforge clarify` to identify gaps in the spec
4. Run `danteforge plan` to generate a detailed execution plan
5. Run `danteforge tasks` to break the plan into executable work
6. Run `danteforge forge 1 --profile quality` to execute the first wave
7. Run `danteforge verify` to confirm the workflow and release state
8. Run `danteforge synthesize` to generate the Ultimate Planning Resource (UPR.md)
